## Summary
<h2>2026.4.27</h2>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>Codex Computer Use setup now ships with status/install commands, marketplace discovery, and fail-closed MCP checks for Codex-mode desktop control. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/pash-openai/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/pash-openai">@pash-openai</a>.</li>
<li>DeepInfra joins the bundled provider set with model discovery, media generation/editing, TTS, embeddings, and provider-owned onboarding policy. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ats3v/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ats3v">@ats3v</a>.</li>
<li>Tencent Yuanbao and QQBot support expand channel coverage with Yuanbao docs/catalog entries and QQBot group chat, streaming, media upload, and pipeline refactors. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/loongfay/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/loongfay">@loongfay</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/cxyhhhhh/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/cxyhhhhh">@cxyhhhhh</a>.</li>
<li>Plugin startup and model catalogs move toward manifest-first metadata, reducing Gateway boot work and making provider rows/aliases/suppressions easier to audit. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li>Reliability fixes cover Telegram startup/sends, Slack socket/media stalls, gateway startup prewarm, session/history defaults, update sync, and Windows restart handoffs. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/joerod26/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/joerod26">@joerod26</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/obviyus/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/obviyus">@obviyus</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shivasymbl/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shivasymbl">@shivasymbl</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/freerk/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/freerk">@freerk</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/bassboy2k/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/bassboy2k">@bassboy2k</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jpreagan/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jpreagan">@jpreagan</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/islandpreneur007/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/islandpreneur007">@islandpreneur007</a>, and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/Thatgfsj/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/Thatgfsj">@Thatgfsj</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Sandbox/Docker: add opt-in <code>sandbox.docker.gpus</code> passthrough for Docker sandbox containers so local GPU workloads can run inside sandboxed agents when the host Docker runtime supports <code>--gpus</code>. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/cyan-ember/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/cyan-ember">@cyan-ember</a>.</li>
<li>iOS/Gateway: add an authenticated <code>node.presence.alive</code> protocol event and <code>node.list</code> last-seen fields so background iOS wakes can mark paired nodes recently alive without treating them as connected. <li>Android: publish authenticated <code>node.presence.alive</code> events after node connect and background transitions so paired Android nodes retain durable last-seen metadata after disconnects. ## Why It Matters
Source signal: <h2>2026.4.27</h2>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>Codex Computer Use setup now ships with status/install commands, marketplace discovery, and fail-closed MCP checks for Codex-mode desktop control. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/pash-openai/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/pash-openai">@pash-openai</a>.</li>

Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ats3v/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ats3v">@ats3v</a>.</li>

<h3>Changes</h3>
